<script>
     function initMobileSwipers() {
          document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel.active .logo-swiper').forEach((swiperEl) => {
               if (!swiperEl.swiper) {
                    new Swiper(swiperEl, {
                         loop: true,
                         autoplay: {
                              delay: 2000,
                              disableOnInteraction: false
                         },
                         slidesPerView: 1.2,
                         breakpoints: {
                              480: { slidesPerView: 2 },
                              768: { slidesPerView: 3 },
                         },
                         spaceBetween: 20,
                         pagination: {
                              el: swiperEl.querySelector('.swiper-pagination'),
                              clickable: true,
                         },
                    });
               }
          });
     }

     function destroyMobileSwipers() {
          document.querySelectorAll('.logo-swiper').forEach((swiperEl) => {
               if (swiperEl.swiper) {
                    swiperEl.swiper.destroy(true, true);
               }
          });
     }

     function handleResize() {
          if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
               initMobileSwipers();
          } else {
               destroyMobileSwipers();
          }
     }

     document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
          handleResize();
          window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);

          document.querySelectorAll('.logo-tabs').forEach(function (module) {
               const buttons = module.querySelectorAll('.filter-tab');
               const panels = module.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel');

               buttons.forEach(function (btn) {
                    btn.addEventListener('click', function () {
                         const target = btn.getAttribute('data-filter');

                         // Update active button
                         buttons.forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
                         btn.classList.add('active');

                         // Toggle panels
                         panels.forEach(p => {
                              const isMatch = p.getAttribute('data-tab-content') === target;
                              p.classList.toggle('active', isMatch);
                         });

                         // Delay ensures DOM changes settle before swiper init
                         setTimeout(handleResize, 300);
                    });
               });
          });
     });
</script></div>

</div><!--end widget-span -->
</div><!--end row-->

                var count = hbspt.targetedContentMetadata.length;
                var targetedContentData = [];
                for (var i = 0; i < count; i++) {

            }

            return metadata;
        };

<script>
     function initSwiper() {
          if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
               document.querySelectorAll('[data-module-id]').forEach(moduleEl => {
                    const hasMobileSlider = moduleEl.getAttribute('data-mobile-slider') === 'true';
                    if (!hasMobileSlider) return;

                    const swiperContainer = moduleEl.querySelector('.swiper-enabled');
                    if (!swiperContainer) return;

                    const paginationEl = moduleEl.querySelector('.swiper-pagination');

                    if (!swiperContainer.classList.contains('swiper-initialized')) {
                         new Swiper(swiperContainer, {
                              slidesPerView: 1,
                              spaceBetween: 20,
                              pagination: {
                                   el: paginationEl,
                                   clickable: true
                              },

                         });

                         // Optional: ensure layout is updated after init
                         setTimeout(() => {
                              swiperContainer.swiper?.update();
                         }, 300);
                    }
               });
          }
     }

     window.addEventListener('load', initSwiper);
     window.addEventListener('resize', initSwiper);
</script>

     <script>
          function initSwiper() {
               if (window.innerWidth <= 1024) {
                    document.querySelectorAll('[data-module-id]').forEach(moduleEl => {
                         const hasMobileSlider = moduleEl.getAttribute('data-mobile-slider') === 'true';
                         if (!hasMobileSlider) return;

                         const swiperContainer = moduleEl.querySelector('.swiper-enabled');
                         if (!swiperContainer) return;

                         const paginationEl = moduleEl.querySelector('.container .swiper-pagination');

                         if (!swiperContainer.classList.contains('swiper-initialized')) {
                              new Swiper(swiperContainer, {
                                   slidesPerView: 1,
                                   spaceBetween: 20,
                                   pagination: {
                                        el: paginationEl,
                                        clickable: true
                                   }
                              });

                              setTimeout(() => {
                                   swiperContainer.swiper?.update();
                              }, 300);
                         }
                    });
               }
          }

         

          // Run Swiper init on page load and resize
          window.addEventListener('load', () => {
               initSwiper();
          });
          window.addEventListener('resize', initSwiper);
     </script>

                     }
                     targetedContentData.push({
                        definitionId: tc[0],
                        criterionId: tc[1],
                        smartTypeId: tc[2]
                     });
                }
                metadata["targetedContentMetadata"] = JSON.stringify(targetedContentData);
            }

            return metadata;
        };

        hbspt.forms.create(options);
    </script>
